     <p class="headline-anim typography-headline large-6 small-12" data-word-anim><span class="color-blue">See the big picture.</span> And all the details.</p> 
     <p class="section-copy display-copy typography-label-alt large-9 medium-10 small-12" data-word-anim>See it all in sharp, glorious detail on the immersive 24?inch 4.5K Retina display.<sup class="footnote footnote-number"><a href="#footnote-3" aria-label="Footnote 2">2</a></sup> The P3 wide color gamut brings what you’re watching to life in over a billion colors. Images shine with a brilliant 500 nits of brightness. Industry-leading anti?reflective coating delivers greater comfort and readability. And True&nbsp;Tone technology automatically adjusts the color temperature of your display to the ambient light of your environment, for a more natural viewing experience. So whether you’re editing photos, working on presentations, or watching your favorite shows and movies, everything looks incredible on&nbsp;iMac.</p>

     </div> 
     <p class="section-copy typography-label-alt large-9 small-11" data-word-anim>It’s the best camera system ever in a Mac. Double the resolution for higher-quality video calls.<sup class="footnote footnote-number"><a href="#footnote-4" aria-label="Footnote 3">3</a></sup> A larger sensor that captures more light. And the advanced image signal processor (ISP) of M1 greatly improves image quality. So from collaborating with coworkers to catching up with friends and family, you’ll always look your best.</p>

    <div class="section-content row"> 
     <div class="column layers-column large-offset-1 large-10 medium-offset-0 medium-12 small-centered" data-component-list="WordAnim" data-start="t - 100vh + 50px" data-anim-type="fade" data-duration="0.6" data-stagger="0.1"> 
      <figure class="layers-figure" data-word-anim> <picture id="overview-photos-1" class="overview-photos" data-lazy>

        <img src="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/photos__n7dv4tf3osq6_large.jpg" onload="__lp(this)" alt> 
       </picture> 
       <noscript> <picture class="overview-photos"> 
         <source srcset="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/photos__n7dv4tf3osq6_small.jpg, /v/imac-24/b/images/overview/photos__n7dv4tf3osq6_small_2x.jpg 2x" media="(max-width:734px)">
         <source srcset="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/photos__n7dv4tf3osq6_medium.jpg, /v/imac-24/b/images/overview/photos__n7dv4tf3osq6_medium_2x.jpg 2x" media="(max-width:1068px)">
         <source srcset="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/photos__n7dv4tf3osq6_large.jpg, /v/imac-24/b/images/overview/photos__n7dv4tf3osq6_large_2x.jpg 2x" media="(min-width:0px)"> 
         <img src="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/photos__n7dv4tf3osq6_large.jpg" alt> 
        </picture> 
       </noscript> 
       <figcaption class="figcaption"> 
        <ul aria-label="The steps taken by the ISP of the M1 chip in iMac to analyze and enhance video:" role="list" class="list typography-caption" data-word-anim> 
         <li role="listitem" class="caption-layer">Auto White Balance</li> 
         <li role="listitem" class="caption-layer">Auto Exposure</li> 
         <li role="listitem" class="caption-layer">Face Detection</li> 
         <li role="listitem" class="caption-layer">Image Fusion</li> 
         <li role="listitem" class="caption-layer">Noise Reduction</li> 
         <li role="listitem" class="caption-layer">Highlight Details</li> 
         <li role="listitem" class="caption-layer">Local Tone Mapping</li> 
        </ul> 
       </figcaption> 
      </figure> 
     </div> 
     <p class="section-copy section-subcopy typography-tout large-10 large-offset-1 medium-offset-0 small-11">The ISP on M1 uses computational video to enhance image quality. To capture stunning video, it goes through a series of steps to analyze and enhance each pixel, at over a trillion operations per second. Advanced noise reduction algorithms bring a new level of clarity. Tone mapping delivers enhanced dynamic range, for more detail in bright highlights and dark shadows. And it works with the Neural Engine in M1 to make more intelligent exposure and white&nbsp;balance adjustments so you look just right in any&nbsp;light.</p> 
    </div> 
   </section> 
   <section class="section section-mics" data-anim-scroll-group="Section - Mics" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:mics"> 
    <div class="section-content row" data-component-list="WordAnim" data-start="t - 100vh + 50px" data-anim-type="fade" data-duration="0.6" data-stagger="0.4"> 
     <div class="headline-anim large-10 medium-12" data-word-anim> 
      <h2 class="section-headline color-purple typography-headline">Studio-quality mics.</h2> 
      <p class="section-subhead typography-headline">For high-quality conversations.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="section-copy typography-label-alt large-10 small-11" data-word-anim>Whether you’re on a video call with a friend, cutting a track, or recording a podcast, the microphones on iMac make sure you come through loud, crisp, and clear. The studio-quality three-mic array is designed to reduce feedback, so conversations flow more naturally&nbsp;and you interrupt each other less. And beamforming technology helps the mics ignore background noise. Which means everyone hears you —&nbsp;not what’s going on around you.</p> 
    </div>

    <div class="spacial-audio-container row"> 
     <p class="typography-label spacial-audio-text column large-6 small-12">The sound system on iMac brings incredible, room-filling audio to any space. Two pairs of force-cancelling woofers create rich, deep bass without unwanted vibrations. And each pair is balanced with a high-performance tweeter. The result is a massive, detailed soundstage that takes your movies, music, and more to the next&nbsp;level.</p> <picture id="overview-speakers-internals-1" class="overview-speakers-internals speakers-internals column large-offset-1 large-5 medium-offset-7 medium-5 small-offset-0 small-12" data-lazy>

     </div> 
     <div class="dolby-atmos-container row"> 
      <p class="typography-label dolby-atmos-text large-7 small-12">Thanks to the redesigned speakers and advanced algorithms, iMac now supports spatial audio when playing video with Dolby Atmos. And when you combine that with the 4.5K Retina display, it’s like bringing the whole theater home.</p>

   <section class="section section-performance" data-anim-scroll-group="Section - Performance" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:m1 and big sur"> 
    <div class="section-content row" data-anchor=".headline-performance-anim" data-component-list="WordAnim" data-start="a0t - 100vh + 200px" data-anim-type="fade" data-duration="0.6" data-stagger="0.4"> 
     <div class="large-12"> <picture id="overview-performance-m1-1" class="overview-performance-m1" data-lazy> 
       <source data-empty srcset="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAHAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw==" media="(min-width:0px)">

      </picture> 
      <noscript> <picture class="overview-performance-m1"> 
        <source srcset="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/performance_m1__c26ffcwest0m_small.jpg, /v/imac-24/b/images/overview/performance_m1__c26ffcwest0m_small_2x.jpg 2x" media="(max-width:734px)">
        <source srcset="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/performance_m1__c26ffcwest0m_medium.jpg, /v/imac-24/b/images/overview/performance_m1__c26ffcwest0m_medium_2x.jpg 2x" media="(max-width:1068px)">
        <source srcset="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/performance_m1__c26ffcwest0m_large.jpg, /v/imac-24/b/images/overview/performance_m1__c26ffcwest0m_large_2x.jpg 2x" media="(min-width:0px)"> 
        <img src="/v/imac-24/b/images/overview/performance_m1__c26ffcwest0m_large.jpg" alt>

     </div> 
     <div class="headline-anim headline-performance-anim large-9 small-12" data-word-anim> 
      <h2 class="section-headline color-pink typography-section-headline">M1 and Big&nbsp;Sur.</h2> 
      <p class="section-subhead typography-section-headline">With great power comes great capability.</p> 
     </div> 
     <p class="section-copy typography-label-alt large-8 medium-10 small-12" data-word-anim>M1 is the most powerful chip we’ve ever made. macOS&nbsp;Big&nbsp;Sur is the most advanced desktop operating system in the world. Combined, they take iMac to entirely new levels of performance, efficiency, and security. iMac wakes from sleep almost instantly, apps launch in a flash, and the whole system feels fluid, smooth, and snappy. With up to 85&nbsp;percent faster CPU performance and up to two times faster graphics performance than standard 21.5?inch&nbsp;iMac models, you can use apps like Xcode and Affinity Photo to compile code in a fraction of the time or edit photos in real time.<sup class="footnote footnote-number"><a href="#footnote-5" aria-label="Footnote 4">4</a></sup> And it runs cool and quiet even while tackling these intense workloads. That’s the power of hardware, software, and silicon —&nbsp;all designed together.</p> 
    </div> 
    <div class="sticky-wrapper performance-sticky-wrapper" data-component-list="PerformanceReveal">

   <section class="section section-continuity" data-anim-scroll-group="Section - Continuity"> 
    <div class="section-content row" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:continuity hero"> 
     <div class="column large-6 medium-8 small-12" data-component-list="WordAnim" data-start="t - 100vh + 200px" data-anim-type="fade" data-duration="0.6" data-stagger="0.4"> 
      <div class="headline-anim" data-word-anim> 
       <h2 class="section-headline color-yellow typography-section-headline">iMac + iPhone.</h2> 
       <p class="section-subhead typography-section-headline">Quite the pair.</p> 
      </div> 
      <p class="section-copy typography-label-alt" data-word-anim>iMac gives you the best of iPhone, on a big, beautiful screen. iPhone lets you access what you need from iMac on the go. And when you use them together, they work like magic.</p> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div class="section-hardware section-hardware-phone align-right" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:continuity phone">

      </div>

    <div class="component-container" data-component-list="AccessoriesKeyboard"> 
     <div class="component-copy-container section-content" data-component-list="WordAnim" data-start="t - 100vh + 50px" data-anim-type="fade" data-duration="0.6" data-stagger="0.4"> 
      <h2 class="visuallyhidden">Color-matched accessories for iMac 24 inches</h2> 
      <p class="accessories-headline typography-headline large-8 medium-9 small-12" data-word-anim>Keep the color going <span class="color-green">all&nbsp;the&nbsp;way&nbsp;to your fingertips. </span></p> 
      <p class="accessories-copy typography-label-alt section-copy large-offset-4 medium-offset-3 small-offset-0" data-word-anim>The new iMac features a color-matched keyboard, mouse, and trackpad. Magic&nbsp;Keyboard now has keys for Spotlight, Dictation, Do Not Disturb, and emoji. And for the first time, Touch&nbsp;ID comes to iMac so you can easily and securely unlock your computer, use Apple&nbsp;Pay, and download apps.<sup class="footnote footnote-number"><a href="#footnote-6" aria-label="Footnote 5">5</a></sup></p> 
     </div>

     <section class="grid-item grid-item-router tile large-span-12 grid-item-environment" data-analytics-section-engagement="name:environment"> 
      <div class="grid-item-header tile-content"> 
       <div class="text-content large-5 large-offset-1 medium-8 medium-offset-0 small-12"> 
        <h2 class="typography-headline grid-item-headline">Designed with the earth in&nbsp;mind.</h2> 
        <p class="grid-item-copy">iMac was designed to minimize its impact on the environment. All of the virgin wood fiber in its packaging comes exclusively from responsibly managed forests. The rare earth elements in the speakers, fan motor, and power connector magnets are completely recycled. And we’re committed to transitioning our entire manufacturing supply chain to 100&nbsp;percent renewable electricity by&nbsp;2030.</p> 
        <p class="grid-item-cta"><a href="/environment/" data-analytics-title="learn more about apple and the environment" class="icon-wrapper"><span class="icon-copy">Learn more about Apple and the&nbsp;environment</span><span class="icon icon-after more"></span></a></p>

      <section class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-column ac-gf-buystrip-info-financing" data-analytics-region="financing"> 
       <div class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-content"> 
        <figure class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-icon ac-gf-buystrip-info-icon-financing"></figure> 
        <h3 class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-title">Get 3% Daily Cash back with Apple&nbsp;Card</h3> 
        <p class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-copy">And pay over time, interest-free when you choose Apple&nbsp;Card Monthly Installments.†</p> <a href="/apple-card/monthly-installments/" class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-cta ac-gf-more" data-analytics-title="apple financing">Learn more</a> 
       </div> 
      </section>

       <div class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-content"> 
        <figure class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-icon ac-gf-buystrip-info-icon-help"></figure> 
        <h3 class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-title">Get help buying</h3> 
        <p class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-copy">Have a question? Call a Specialist or chat online.</p> 
        <p class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-caption">Call 1-800-MY-APPLE.</p> <a href="https://contactretail.apple.com/?pg=COM:imac-24&amp;ap=COM&amp;c=us&amp;l=en" class="ac-gf-buystrip-info-cta ac-gf-buystrip-info-cta-chat ac-gf-more" data-analytics-title="get help buying" data-analytics-exit-link>Contact us</a> 
       </div> 
      </section>
